	window.addEventListener("unload", deleteTracking, false);

	function deleteTracking(){
		localStorage.removeItem("tracking_"+"home");
	}


	function comportamiento(tipo, social, pagina, id){
		var pagina_url = 'https://www.elsalvador.com';
		var term_id = '';
		var tag_nombre = '';
		var tag_slug = '';
		var id_wp = '';
		var tag_principal_term_id = '';
		var tag_principal_name = '';
		var tag_principal_slug = '';
		if(tipo == "share"){
			pagina_url = pagina;
			term_id = '';
			tag_nombre = '';
			tag_slug = '';
			tag_principal_term_id = '';
			tag_principal_name = '';
			tag_principal_slug = '';
			id_wp = id;
		}
		var referrer = document.referrer;
		var comportamiento={
			id_cookie: localStorage.getItem("cookie_dispositivo"),
			pagina_url: pagina_url,
			tipo: tipo,
			social: social,
			referrer: referrer,
			term_id: term_id,
			tag_nombre: tag_nombre,
			tag_slug: tag_slug,
			id_wp: id_wp,
			tiempo_nota: 0,
			tag_principal_term_id: tag_principal_term_id,
			tag_principal_name: tag_principal_name,
			tag_principal_slug: tag_principal_slug,
			metodo: 'save_comportamiento'
		};
		$.ajax({
			type: "post",
			url: 'https://back-search.elsalvador.com/comportamiento/save_comportamiento',
			//dataType: 'json',
			data: JSON.stringify(comportamiento),
			contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
			success: function(respuesta) {
				if(tipo == 'pageview'){
					localStorage.setItem("tracking_"+"home", respuesta);
				}
            }
		});
	}
	
	function dispositivo(tipo){
		var navegador = navigator.userAgent;
		var d = new Date();
		var fecha_hora = d.getTime();
		var hash =  Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 15) +Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 15)+ fecha_hora;
		localStorage.setItem("cookie_dispositivo", hash);
		var dispositivo={
			navegador: navegador,
			id_cookie: hash,
			metodo: 'save_dispositivo'
		};	
		$.ajax({
			type: "post",
			url: 'https://back-search.elsalvador.com/comportamiento/save_dispositivo',
			data: JSON.stringify(dispositivo),
			contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8'	
			}).done(function(response){
				if(response != false){
					comportamiento(tipo);
					document.getElementById('historico').src = "https://historico.elsalvador.com/historico/seguimiento.html?metodo=save&key=cookie_dispositivo&value="+hash;
				}
		});
	}
$(document).ready(function(){
	var id_cookie = localStorage.getItem("cookie_dispositivo");
	var tipo = "pageview";
	if(id_cookie == null){
		dispositivo(tipo);
	}else{
		comportamiento(tipo);	
	}   
});

			function validate(){
			  var s = document.getElementById("s").value; 	
			  if(!s || s.length < 3){ //la clave de busqueda debe poseer al menos 3 caracteres
			    document.getElementById("s_error").style.display = 'inline-block';
			  }else if(s.length > 30){ //la clave de busqueda no debe exceder de 30 caracteres 
			    document.getElementById("s_error2").style.display = 'inline-block';
			  }else{
			    document.forms['searching'].submit();	
			  }	
			  setTimeout(function(){
	            document.getElementById("s_error").style.display = 'none';
			    document.getElementById("s_error2").style.display = 'none';
			  }, 3000);
			}
		//***************************************** FIN SEARCHFORM **********************************

				function cargarDatosAjax(element, response) {
					if (document.getElementById("data4").value == "true") {
						var ajaxUrl = "https://www.elsalvador.com/wp-json/LoadMore/v1/load";
					  	var id = element.attr('id');

					  	var html_banner = document.getElementById(porciones[0]+'-banner').value;
					  	var data = doc
10f8
ument.getElementById("data").value;

						var data3 = document.getElementById("data3").value;

				  			html_banner:html_banner,

						  	idAds:data,
						  	idAds2:data2,
						  	idAds3:data3

			<script type="text/javascript">
           
              $(document).ready(function(){
                var url_base = "https://www.elsalvador.com/wp-json/LoadMore/v1/getTopHotTrend";

                function loadTopContent(type){
                  $.ajax({
                    url: url_base + "/" + type,
                    method: "GET",
                    dataType: "json"
                  }).done(function(data){
                  	 switch(type){
                  	   case 1:
                  	           $("#top-content-box").html(data);
                  	           break;
                  	   case 2:
                  	           $("#hot-content-box").html(data);
                  	           break;
                  	   case 3:
                  	           $("#trending-content-box").html(data);
                  	           break;   	
                  	 }
                  }).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown){
                     console.log("Error al obtener las notas del top: " + JSON.stringify(jqXHR));
                  });
                }

                loadTopContent(1);
                  
                $("#hot-link").on("click
336
", function(){
                   if(!$.trim($("#hot-content-box").html())){
                     loadTopContent(2);
                   }	
                });

                $("#trending-link").on("click", function(){
                   if(!$.trim($("#trending-content-box").html())){
                     loadTopContent(3);
                   }
                });


              });

            </script>
